## Codebase Exploration Report: Neural Image Foundation - 4M Training System

### **1. Full Contents of Key Files**

#### **run_scaling_experiment_2.py** (Lines 1-551)
**Path:** `/home/users/liubr/projects/neural-image-foundation/neural-foundation-model/ml-4m/run_scaling_experiment_2.py`

This is a Chinchilla Scaling Law pipeline that conducts a two-part experiment:
- **Part 1 (Sweep):** Launches training across a grid of model dimensions and token counts
- **Part 2 (Fit):** Fits scaling laws using the chinchilla package

**Key Components:**
- **Sweep Grid (lines 37-62):** Configures model sizes (dim 128-512) and token counts (5B tokens), with support for 2-3 layer variants
- **Config Generation (lines 83-131):** Generates YAML configs dynamically, patches model dimensions, handles test runs
- **Training Launch (lines 138-165):** Runs `torchrun` with `run_training_4m.py` using subprocess
- **Result Collection (lines 202-305):** Parses training logs (JSON format) to extract losses for both RGB and depth modalities
- **Scaling Law Fit (lines 312-405):** Uses Chinchilla to fit L(N,D) = E + A/N^alpha + B/D^beta
- **Plotting (lines 412-477):** Generates loss curves vs. model size and data scale
- **Main execution (lines 526-551):** CLI with modes: sweep, fit, collect, all

Main training script for 4M model using Distributed Data Parallel (DDP):

   - Returns: `modality_info`, `data_loader_train`, `num_training_steps_per_epoch`, validation loaders

3. **Model Creation (lines 354-387):**
   - Creates encoder/decoder embeddings per modality
   - Instantiates FourM model via `create_model()`
   - Supports modality filtering (in_domains, out_domains)

4. **Training Loop (lines 390-677):**
   - DDP setup with `init_distributed_mode()`
   - Epoch-based training with gradient accumulation
   - Learning rate scheduling (cosine or inverse sqrt with warmup/cooldown)
   - Weight decay scheduling
   - Loss scaling for mixed precision
   - Checkpoint saving every N epochs
   - JSON-formatted logging to `log.txt`

5. **Loss Computation - `train_one_epoch()` (lines 680-804):**
   - Iterates over batches
   - Forward pass: `model(mod_dict, num_encoder_tokens, num_decoder_tokens, loss_type)`
   - Returns: `loss` (scalar) and `mod_loss` (dict per modality)
   - Gradient accumulation with optional gradient clipping/skipping
   - Per-step metrics: loss, per-modality loss, learning rate, weight decay, gradient norm

6. **Evaluation - `evaluate()` (lines 807-843):**
   - No-grad evaluation mode
   - Computes loss on validation/fixed eval sets
   - Returns per-modality losses with prefix (e.g., "[Fixed Eval (cc12m)] tok_rgb@224_loss")

### **3. Model Architecture and Training Loop**

#### **FourM Model Class** (fourm/models/fm.py, lines 62-845)

**Architecture:**
- **Encoder:** Stack of transformer blocks with multi-head attention
  - Input: Embedded tokens from multiple modalities (RGB, depth, neural, etc.)
  - Output: Context tokens
  
- **Decoder:** Stack of transformer blocks with cross-attention to encoder
  - Input: Mask tokens (for images) or shifted sequences (for text)
  - Attention modes: Causal (autoregressive), per-modality separation
  - Output: Logits for each modality's vocabulary

**Key Methods:**

1. **Forward Masking:**
   - `forward_mask_encoder()` (lines 346-398): Selects `num_encoder_tokens` from all modalities, adds register tokens
   - `forward_mask_decoder()` (lines 400-446): Selects `num_decoder_tokens`, prepares targets for loss

2. **Forward Pass** (lines 648-699):
   ```
   mod_dict (multi-modality input)
     ↓
   encoder_embeddings[mod](d) → get encoder tokens + embeddings
     ↓
   forward_mask_encoder(num_encoder_tokens) → selected encoder tokens
     ↓
   forward_encoder(tokens + embeddings) → context
     ↓
   decoder_embeddings[mod].forward_embed(d) → decoder tokens + embeddings
     ↓
   forward_mask_decoder(num_decoder_tokens) → selected decoder tokens + targets
     ↓
   forward_decoder(tokens + embeddings, context) → decoder output
     ↓
   forward_loss(decoder_output, targets) → loss + per-modality losses
   ```

3. **Loss Computation** (lines 555-645):
   - **Modality-wise loss** (`forward_mod_loss`, lines 581-610):
     - Computes cross-entropy per modality: `F.cross_entropy(logits, target_ids)`
     - Averages per-modality losses: `loss = mean([loss_rgb, loss_depth, ...])`
   
   - **Token-wise loss** (`forward_token_loss`, lines 612-645):
     - Weights each modality's loss by token count
     - `loss = sum([loss_mod * count_mod]) / total_count`

**Modality System:**
- Each modality has an ID, encoder/decoder embeddings
- Supports flexible in/out domains (e.g., RGB+depth→RGB)
- Attention masks can be causal or per-modality-separated

### **4. Key Training Flows**

**Epoch Loop (run_training_4m.py, lines 604-677):**
```
for epoch in range(start_epoch, epochs):
    train_one_epoch(...) → train_stats
    if (epoch+1) % eval_freq == 0:
        for val_loader in data_loaders_val:
            evaluate(model, val_loader) → eval_stats
    log_stats.update(train_stats + eval_stats)
    if (epoch+1) % save_freq == 0:
        save_checkpoint()
    write_log.txt(json.dumps(log_stats))
```

**Batch Loop (lines 703-791):**
```
for step, batch in enumerate(data_loader):
    # Prepare batch
    mod_dict = {mod: {k: v.to(device) for ...}}
    
    # Forward + loss
    loss, mod_loss = model(mod_dict, num_input_tokens, num_target_tokens, loss_type)
    
    # Backward + gradient accumulation
    loss = loss / accum_iter
    loss_scaler(loss, optimizer, clip_grad, skip_grad)
    
    if (step+1) % accum_iter == 0:
        optimizer.step()
        optimizer.zero_grad()
    
    # Log metrics
    log_writer.update({loss, mod_loss, lr, grad_norm, ...})
```

**Result Collection (lines 252-305):**
- Parses `checkpoints/log.txt` (JSON lines)
- Extracts `[Fixed Eval (dataset)] tok_rgb@224_loss` and `tok_depth@224_loss`
- Collects at 3 checkpoints: 1/3, 2/3, final epoch
- Filters for ≥1B tokens seen
- Saves to `results.json` with fields: run, dim, N (params), layers, total_tokens, D (tokens), loss_rgb, loss_depth

**Scaling Law Fit:**
- Uses Chinchilla: L(N,D) = E + A/N^alpha + B/D^beta
- Parameter search grid:
  - E: [6.0-9.0] (irreducible loss floor)
  - A, B: [100-2200] (coefficients)
  - alpha, beta: [0.05-0.5], [0.1-0.5] (exponents)

### **7. Key Implementation Details**

**Token Counting:**
- Input tokens: num_input_tokens (default 128)
- Target tokens: num_target_tokens (default 128)
- Total tokens per sample: 256
- Epochs computed as: `ceil(total_tokens_B * 1e9 / (input+target_tokens * epoch_size))`

**Loss Reporting:**
- Log format: JSON per line with structure:
  ```json
  {
    "total_tokens_seen_b": 5.2,
    "[Fixed Eval (cc12m)] tok_rgb@224_loss": 8.123,
    "[Fixed Eval (cc12m)] tok_depth@224_loss": 7.456,
    ...
  }
  ```

**Model Parameter Estimation:**
- Not explicitly computed in sweep, extracted from training logs
- Parsing line: "Number of params: X M"

### 3. DATA LOADING CODE: Train vs Val Distinction

**Key Files:**
- `/home/users/liubr/projects/neural-image-foundation/neural-foundation-model/ml-4m/fourm/data/pretrain_utils.py` (lines 84-184 for train, 195-292 for val)
- `/home/users/liubr/projects/neural-image-foundation/neural-foundation-model/ml-4m/fourm/data/unified_datasets.py` (lines 319-395 for WDS dataloader, 48-90 for regular dataset)
- `/home/users/liubr/projects/neural-image-foundation/neural-foundation-model/ml-4m/run_training_4m.py` (lines 293-344 for instantiation)

**Train Dataloader Construction:**
- **File:** `fourm/data/pretrain_utils.py`, lines 84-184
- **Function:** `get_train_dataloader()`
- **Logic:**
  - If `dataset_config['use_wds'] == True`: Calls `build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader()` (lines 125-140)
    - Uses webdataset for large training datasets with sharded tar files
    - Supports multi-modal data with `wds_n_repeats`, shuffle buffers for tar loading and repeat shuffling
  - If `use_wds == False`: Calls `build_fm_pretraining_dataset()` (lines 142-158)
    - Creates standard PyTorch Dataset from filesystem
    - Wraps with DistributedSampler for multi-GPU training
    - Single-worker DataLoader with batch_size=1, then collated through Mixture dataloader

**Val Dataloader Construction:**
- **File:** `fourm/data/pretrain_utils.py`, lines 195-292
- **Function:** `get_val_dataloader()`
- **Logic:**
  - For `dataset_type == 'multimodal'` (lines 212-263):
    - **ALWAYS uses `build_fm_pretraining_dataset()`** (line 240) - NOT webdataset
    - Uses CenterCropImageAugmenter (no augmentation) for evaluation
    - Creates standard PyTorch DataLoader with DistributedSampler or SequentialSampler
    - Respects `fixed_eval` flag for fixed token ranges
  - For `dataset_type == 'huggingface'` (lines 265-287):
    - Calls `build_huggingface_pretraining_dataloader()` - different path than WDS
    - Still not WDS format, but uses HuggingFace datasets API

**CRITICAL FINDING:** Validation dataloaders **CANNOT use webdataset format**. The `get_val_dataloader()` function explicitly ignores the `use_wds` config setting and always uses `build_fm_pretraining_dataset()` which requires folder-based data layout, not tar shards. This is documented in line 54-55 of `unified_datasets.py`: "This function should mainly used for smaller datasets (e.g. validation sets), while large training sets should be loaded with build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader in webdataset format."

**WebDataset Pipeline Details:**
- **File:** `fourm/data/unified_datasets.py`, lines 319-395
- **Function:** `build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader()`
- Pipeline stages (lines 370-385):
  1. ResampledShards: Sample shards from brace-expanded paths
  2. multi_tarfile_samples: Extract samples from tar files
  3. shuffle (tar buffer): Shuffle after loading
  4. wds_decoder: Decode bytes to images/arrays
  5. repeat_fn: Repeat samples n times
  6. shuffle (repeat buffer): Shuffle after repeating
  7. remove_extensions: Clean key names
  8. filter_metadata: Remove non-task keys
  9. tok_to_int64: Convert tokens
  10. rename_modalities: Map to modality names
  11. transform: Apply augmentation + masking
  12. batched: Batch with collation_fn

**Train/Val Data Path Distinction (from configs):**
- Train: Use `shard-{00000..00052}.tar` webdataset shards with `use_wds: True`
- Val: Use folder paths like `/project/data/val/cc12m` with `use_wds: False`

---

### How Modalities are Registered & Handled

**Modality Registration (modality_info.py):**
- All modalities are defined in a global `MODALITY_INFO` dictionary with entries for each modality
- Each modality entry contains:
  - `type`: 'img', 'seq', 'seq_emb', or 'seq_token'
  - `encoder_embedding`: Function to instantiate encoder (e.g., `ImageTokenEncoderEmbedding`)
  - `decoder_embedding`: Function to instantiate decoder
  - `min_tokens`/`max_tokens`: Token budget constraints
  - `vocab_size`: For tokenized modalities
  - `id`: Unique modality identifier (hashed)
  - `path`: Path pattern for loading data
  - `pretokenized`: Boolean flag if pre-tokenized

**Example modality entries:**
- `tok_rgb@224`: Tokenized RGB images (224x224), vocab_size 16384, 196 max tokens
- `tok_depth@224`: Tokenized depth maps, vocab_size 8192, 196 max tokens
- `caption`: Text sequences, vocab_size 30000, 256 max tokens

**Encoder/Decoder Initialization (run_training_4m.py lines 359-377):**
```python
encoder_embeddings = {}
for mod in args.all_domains:
    info = modality_info[mod]
    # Image-like modalities need patch_size and image_size
    if 'patch_size' in signature(info["encoder_embedding"]).parameters:
        encoder_embeddings[mod] = info["encoder_embedding"](patch_size=patch_size, image_size=image_size)
    else:
        encoder_embeddings[mod] = info["encoder_embedding"]()

decoder_embeddings = {} # Same process for decoder
```

Each modality embedding module is instantiated via a `partial()` function from modality_info, then its `init()` method is called with the model's embedding dimension.

---

### Scaling Model Config Files

**4m-neural-2e-2d-scaling.yaml:**

```yaml
# Architecture
model: fm_neural_2e_2d_gelu
patch_size: 16
input_size: 224
dtype: bfloat16

# Training
num_input_tokens: 256
num_target_tokens: 256
loss_type: mod  # Per-modality loss
epochs: -1 (uses total_tokens instead)
total_tokens: 5  # billion
batch_size: 64  # 64 x 64 GPUs = 4096

# Data
data_config: "cfgs/neural/4m/modal/data/rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml"
alphas_config uses rgb2depth-all2all-no-neural.yaml

# Model: 2 encoder + 2 decoder layers, 128-320 hidden dims
```

**4m-neural-3e-3d-scaling.yaml:**
```yaml
# Same as above but:
model: fm_neural_3e_3d_gelu  # 3 encoder + 3 decoder
```

Both configs reference the Dirichlet alpha mixture config: `/home/users/liubr/projects/neural-image-foundation/neural-foundation-model/ml-4m/cfgs/neural/4m/modal/alphas_mixture/rgb2depth-all2all-no-neural.yaml`

This specifies token budget mixing for RGB→depth and all-to-all tasks.

---

### How Missing Modalities are Handled During Training

**Key Handling Point (masking.py line 548):**
```python
mod_name_load = mod_name if mod_name in mod_dict else get_transform_key(mod_name)
```

This is the critical line that handles missing modalities:

1. **Graceful Fallback:** If a modality is not present in the sample's mod_dict, the code attempts to load it using just the base name (e.g., `'tok_rgb'` instead of `'tok_rgb@224'`)

2. **Dirichlet Sampling:** Token budgets are sampled per-modality using Dirichlet distributions (masking.py lines 160-165). The alphas config can set very low alpha values (~0) for modalities that should rarely appear in the input or target.

3. **Input/Target Masking:** For each modality, the code calls the appropriate masking function (`image_mask`, `sequence_mask`, etc.) with:
   - `input_budget`: Tokens to keep in encoder (sampled from Dirichlet)
   - `target_budget`: Tokens to predict in decoder (sampled from Dirichlet)
   
   A modality can be **completely masked out** by setting its sampled budget to 0.

4. **Modality Mask Tracking:** The FourM model tracks which tokens belong to which modality using `mod_mask` (fm.py line 278):
   ```python
   mod_mask_all.append(torch.full_like(d['input_mask'], 
                                      self.modality_info[mod]['id'], 
                                      dtype=torch.int16))
   ```
   This allows the decoder to maintain modality-separate attention masks if `decoder_sep_mask=True` (fm.py line 109).

5. **Token Budget Constraints:** Each modality respects `min_tokens` and `max_tokens` from MODALITY_INFO. Sampling ensures:
   - No modality gets fewer than min_tokens
   - No modality exceeds max_tokens

---

### Pattern for Adding Neural Recording Modality

To add a neural recording modality (e.g., 10% sparsity scenario), you would:

1. **Add to modality_info.py:**
```python
'tok_neural@224': {
    'input_size': 224,
    'patch_size': 16,
    'vocab_size': 8192,  # or appropriate codebook size
    'encoder_embedding': partial(ImageTokenEncoderEmbedding, vocab_size=8192),
    'decoder_embedding': partial(ImageTokenDecoderEmbedding, vocab_size=8192),
    'min_tokens': 0,
    'max_tokens': None,  # Set to 196 at runtime
    'type': 'img',
    'id': generate_uint15_hash('tok_neural@224'),
    'pretokenized': True,
}
```

2. **Add to alphas_config (rgb2depth-all2all-no-neural.yaml):**
```yaml
tok_neural@224:
  input_alphas: [0., 0.5]   # 0% in rgb2all, 50% in all2all
  target_alphas: [0.5, 0.5] # 50% in both modes
```

   For 10% sparsity, you'd set alphas very low or use a separate mixture with low weight.

3. **Update data_config to include tok_neural:**
```yaml
data_path: '/path/[tok_rgb@224,tok_depth@224,tok_neural@224,crop_settings]/shard-{00000..00052}.tar'
```

4. **The masking system automatically handles sparse data:** If a sample lacks the neural modality, line 548 in masking.py will attempt to load it, but the Dirichlet sampling ensures it only gets a small token budget anyway, or the training can skip it entirely based on alphas.

---

### Summary

The FourM architecture is highly modular with automatic multi-modal handling:
- **Modalities registered** in a centralized MODALITY_INFO dictionary
- **Encoder/Decoder embeddings** instantiated dynamically per modality
- **Token budgets sampled** from Dirichlet mixtures (configured via YAML)
- **Missing modalities** gracefully skipped with fallback name resolution
- **Modality masks** tracked for attention constraints and per-modality loss computation
- **Scaling configs** provided for different model sizes (2e-2d to 24e-24d)
- **Data configs** specify which modalities to load and their mixing strategy

This design naturally supports sparse/missing modalities without code changes—just adjust the Dirichlet alphas in the config YAML.

261	
262	        for total_tokens in token_configs:
263	            run_name = make_run_name(dim, layers, total_tokens)
264	            run_dir  = sweep_output_dir / run_name
265	            if test_run:
266	                run_dir = run_dir / "test_run"
267	
268	            # D    = int(total_tokens * 1e9)   # convert B tokens → raw count
269	            losses = extract_final_loss(run_dir, test_run)
270	            N = extract_model_size(run_dir, test_run)
271	
272	            if len(losses) > 0:
273	                indices = set([
274	                    len(losses) // 3,
275	                    2 * len(losses) // 3,
276	                    len(losses) - 1,
277	                ])
278	                for i, loss in enumerate(losses):
279	                    if i not in indices:
280	                        continue
281	                    total_tokens_seen = loss["total_tokens_seen_b"]
282	                    if total_tokens_seen < 1.0:
283	                        continue
284	
285	                    results.append({
286	                        "run":          run_name,
287	                        "dim":          dim,
288	                        "N":            N,
289	                        "layers":       layers,
290	                        "total_tokens": loss["total_tokens_seen_b"],
291	                        "D":            loss["total_tokens_seen_b"] * 1e9,
292	                        "loss_rgb":     loss["[Fixed Eval (cc12m)] tok_rgb@224_loss"],
293	                        "loss_depth":   loss["[Fixed Eval (cc12m)] tok_depth@224_loss"]
294	                    })
295	                # print(f"  {run_name}: N={N:,}  D={D:,}  losses={losses:}")
296	            else:
297	                print(f"  {run_name}: INCOMPLETE — skipping")
298	
299	    # Save results
300	    sweep_output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
301	    with open(results_file, "w") as f:
302	        json.dump(results, f, indent=2)
303	
304	    print(f"\nSaved {len(results)} results to {results_file}")
305	    return results
306	
307	
308	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
309	# 6. SCALING LAW FIT
310	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
311	
312	def fit_scaling_law(results, sweep_output_dir, condition, loss_type="rgb"):
313	    """
314	    Fit L(N, D) = E + A/N^alpha + B/D^beta using the chinchilla package.
315	 
316	    Key API facts from source:
317	      - cc.append(N, D, loss) adds a data point to the internal database
318	      - D is number of IMAGE SAMPLES, not tokens — convert from tokens
319	      - cc.fit() runs BFGS over param_grid to find best (E, A, B, alpha, beta)
320	      - cc.report() prints fitted params and goodness of fit
321	      - cc.predict_loss(N, D) gives predicted loss after fitting
322	    """
323	    try:
324	        from chinchilla import Chinchilla
325	    except ImportError:
326	        print("Install chinchilla: pip install git+https://github.com/kyo-takano/chinchilla.git")
327	        return
328	 
329	    if len(results) < 3:
330	        print(f"Only {len(results)} results — chinchilla needs at least 3 to fit")
331	        return
332	 
333	    print(f"\nFitting scaling law on {len(results)} points...")
334	 
335	    N_values    = [r["N"]    for r in results]
336	    # D in chinchilla is samples, not tokens
337	    # Convert: tokens / (num_input_tokens + num_target_tokens) = samples seen
338	    # Use total_tokens * 1e9 / tokens_per_sample as effective sample count
339	    # If you don't know tokens_per_sample exactly, use raw token count — 
340	    # it shifts B but not beta, which is what you care about comparatively
341	    if loss_type == "rgb":
342	        loss_key = "loss_rgb"
343	    elif loss_type == "depth":
344	        loss_key = "loss_depth"
345	    else:
346	        raise RuntimeError(f"Bad loss type: {loss_type}")
347	    D_values    = [r["D"]    for r in results]  # already in raw tokens from collect_results
348	    loss_values = [r[loss_key] for r in results]
349	 
350	    print(f"  N range:    {min(N_values):,} – {max(N_values):,}")
351	    print(f"  D range:    {min(D_values):,.0f} – {max(D_values):,.0f}")
352	    print(f"  Loss range: {min(loss_values):.4f} – {max(loss_values):.4f}")
353	 
354	    # Initialize Chinchilla — no seed_ranges needed since we're only fitting,
355	    # not using it to suggest next runs
356	    cc = Chinchilla(
357	        project_dir=str(sweep_output_dir / f"chinchilla_db_{loss_type}"),
358	 
359	        param_grid=dict(
360	            # E: irreducible loss floor — set below your best observed loss
361	            # Your epoch 27 loss was ~8.0, still improving, so floor ~5-7
362	            E=np.linspace(6.0, 9, 5),
363	 
364	            # A, B: penalty coefficients — scale with your loss magnitude (~8-9)
365	            # With N~11M and alpha~0.2: A/N^0.2 ~ A/27, so A~hundreds to be meaningful
366	            A=np.linspace(100, 2200, 5),
367	            B=np.linspace(100, 2200, 5),
368	 
369	            # alpha, beta: scaling exponents
370	            # Vision tends lower than language (Chinchilla found ~0.34 for text)
371	            # Embedding-heavy models like yours may have even lower alpha
372	            alpha=np.linspace(0.05, 0.4, 5),
373	            beta=np.linspace(0.1,  0.5, 5),
374	        ),
375	    )
376	 
377	    # Load all results into chinchilla's database
378	    # append() signature from source: cc.append(N=N, D=D, loss=loss)
379	    for r in results:
380	        cc.append(N=r["N"], D=r["D"], loss=r[loss_key])
381	 
382	    print(f"\nLoaded {len(results)} data points into chinchilla database")
383	 
384	    # Fit — runs BFGS over all param_grid combinations in parallel
385	    # Minimum 3 points required (enforced in source)
386	    cc.fit(parallel=True)
387	 
388	    # Report — prints fitted params + goodness of fit via loss_fn (asymmetric_mae)
389	    cc.report(plot=True)  # set plot=False if no display available (e.g. on cluster)
390	 
391	    # Save fitted params manually as well
392	    try:
393	        params = cc.get_params()
394	        params["condition"] = condition
395	        params["n_points"]  = len(results)
396	        fit_path = sweep_output_dir / "scaling_law_fit.json"
397	        with open(fit_path, "w") as f:
398	            json.dump(params, f, indent=2)
399	        print(f"\nFit saved to {fit_path}")
400	        print(f"\nFitted scaling law:")
401	        print(f"  L(N,D) = {params['E']:.4f} + {params['A']:.4f}/N^{params['alpha']:.4f} + {params['B']:.4f}/D^{params['beta']:.4f}")
402	    except ValueError as e:
403	        print(f"Could not save params: {e}")
404	 
405	    return cc
406	
407	
408	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
409	# 7. PLOTTING
410	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
411	
412	def plot_results(results, sweep_output_dir, model_configs, condition, law=None, loss_type="rgb"):
413	    """Basic loss curve plots for qualitative scaling observations."""
414	    try:
415	        import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
416	        import numpy as np
417	    except ImportError:
418	        print("pip install matplotlib numpy for plotting")
419	        return
420	
421	    fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(12, 5))
422	    fig.suptitle(f"Scaling Laws — {condition}")
423	
424	    colors = ["#2196F3", "#FF5722", "#4CAF50"]
425	
426	    # Left: loss vs D (tokens), one line per model size
427	    ax = axes[0]
428	    for i, model_cfg in enumerate(model_configs):
429	        dim = model_cfg["dim"]
430	        layers = model_cfg["layers"]
431	        pts = [(r["D"], r[f"loss_{loss_type}"]) for r in results if r["dim"] == dim]
432	        for r in results:
433	            if r["dim"] == dim and r["layers"] == layers:
434	                N = r["N"]
435	                break
436	
437	        if not pts:
438	            continue
439	        pts.sort()
440	        D_pts, L_pts = zip(*pts)
441	        # N = count_parameters(dim, model_cfg["num_heads"])
442	        ax.plot(D_pts, L_pts, "o-", color=colors[i], label=f"dim={dim} (N≈{N/1e6:.1f}M)")
443	
444	    ax.set_xlabel("Tokens seen (D)")
445	    ax.set_ylabel("Validation loss")
446	    ax.set_title("Loss vs. Data Scale")
447	    ax.set_xscale("log")
448	    ax.legend()
449	    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
450	
451	    # Right: loss vs N (params), one line per token budget
452	    ax = axes[1]
453	    token_colors = ["#9C27B0", "#00BCD4", "#FF9800"]
454	    for i, total_tokens in enumerate(TOKEN_CONFIGS):
455	        pts = [
456	            (r["model_size"],
457	             r["loss"])
458	            for r in results if r["total_tokens"] == total_tokens
459	        ]
460	        if not pts:
461	            continue
462	        pts.sort()
463	        N_pts, L_pts = zip(*pts)
464	        ax.plot(N_pts, L_pts, "s-", color=token_colors[i], label=f"{total_tokens}B tokens")
465	
466	    ax.set_xlabel("Parameters (N)")
467	    ax.set_ylabel("Validation loss")
468	    ax.set_title("Loss vs. Model Scale")
469	    ax.set_xscale("log")
470	    ax.legend()
471	    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)
472	
473	    plt.tight_layout()
474	    plot_path = sweep_output_dir / "scaling_curves.png"
475	    plt.savefig(plot_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches="tight")
476	    print(f"Plot saved to {plot_path}")
477	    plt.show()
478

480	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
481	# 8. MAIN
482	# ─────────────────────────────────────────────
483	
484	def run_sweep(model_configs, train_token_configs, sweep_output_dir, condition, test_run=False):
485	    """Launch all training runs sequentially."""
486	    print(f"Starting sweep: {len(model_configs)} model sizes x {len(train_token_configs)} token counts")
487	    print(f"Condition: {condition}\n")
488	
489	    for model_cfg in model_configs:
490	        for total_tokens in train_token_configs:
491	            dim       = model_cfg["dim"]
492	            num_heads = model_cfg["num_heads"]
493	            layers = model_cfg["layers"]
494	            run_name  = make_run_name(dim, layers, total_tokens)
495	
496	            print(f"\n{'='*50}")
497	            print(f"Run: {run_name}  (dim={dim}, {total_tokens}B tokens)")
498	            print(f"{'='*50}")
499	
500	            model_cfg_path, run_dir = generate_configs(
501	                dim, layers, num_heads, total_tokens, sweep_output_dir, test_run
502	            )
503	            launch_training(model_cfg_path, run_dir)
504	
505	    print("\nSweep complete. Run with --mode fit to analyze results.")
506	
507	
508	def run_fit(results_file, sweep_output_dir, condition, test_run=False, loss_type="rgb"):
509	    """Collect results and fit scaling law."""
510	    # if not results_file.exists():
511	    #     print("Collecting results from training logs...")
512	    #     results = collect_results(test_run)
513	    # else:
514	    print(f"Loading existing results from {results_file}")
515	    with open(results_file) as f:
516	        results = json.load(f)
517	
518	    if not results:
519	        print("No results found. Run sweep first, then collect, then fit.")
520	        return
521	
522	    law = fit_scaling_law(results, sweep_output_dir, condition, loss_type)
523	    plot_results(results, law, loss_type)
524	
525	
526	if __name__ == "__main__":
527	    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
528	    parser.add_argument(
529	        "--mode",
530	        choices=["sweep", "fit", "collect", "all"],
531	        default="all",
532	        help="sweep: run training; fit: analyze results; collect: just parse logs; all: both"
533	    )
534	    parser.add_argument(
535	        "--test_run",
536	        default=False
537	    )
538	    parser.add_argument("--loss_type", choices=["rgb", "depth"], type=str, default="rgb")
539	    args = parser.parse_args()
540	    test_run = args.test_run
541	    loss_type = args.loss_type
542	    if args.mode == "sweep":
543	        run_sweep(MODEL_CONFIGS, TRAIN_TOKEN_CONFIGS, SWEEP_OUTPUT_DIR, CONDITION, test_run)
544	    elif args.mode == "fit":
545	        run_fit(RESULTS_FILE, SWEEP_OUTPUT_DIR, CONDITION, test_run, loss_type)
546	    elif args.mode == "collect":
547	        collect_results(RESULTS_FILE, SWEEP_OUTPUT_DIR, MODEL_CONFIGS, TOKEN_CONFIGS, test_run)
548	    elif args.mode == "all":
549	        run_sweep(MODEL_CONFIGS, TRAIN_TOKEN_CONFIGS, SWEEP_OUTPUT_DIR, CONDITION, test_run)
550	        collect_results(RESULTS_FILE, SWEEP_OUTPUT_DIR, MODEL_CONFIGS, TOKEN_CONFIGS, test_run)
551	        run_fit(RESULTS_FILE, test_run, loss_type)

33	        spec.loader.exec_module(loader)
34	        return loader.load_modal_image()
35	    raise ImportError("_modal_load.py not found (expected /opt/repo/4m_training on Modal)")

The config is trying to use 512 dimensions with a 2-layer architecture, which doesn't exist in the registered models. I'm realizing there's a problem with how the losses list is being populated—it includes every log line, not just the eval epochs, so the index-based sampling strategy might be pulling from training lines that don't have the eval metrics at all. The issue gets more complicated because not every epoch necessarily runs evaluation.

With eval_freq: 1, every epoch should have eval stats, but in small test runs with only a few epochs, the indices calculated by dividing the list length into thirds could overlap or point to the same entries. The code handles this by converting to a set to deduplicate, then filters further by checking that each checkpoint has at least 1 billion tokens seen before extracting the loss values.

But there's a potential issue with how the training logs are being sampled—the script logs one JSON line per epoch, and the collection function is trying to sample at 1/3, 2/3, and final positions.

With the given parameters, there would be about 33 epochs total, meaning roughly 33 logged lines. The sampling would target indices around 11, 22, and 32 for the three checkpoints. For the test run with much smaller parameters, the filter would likely discard all results since it wouldn't accumulate enough tokens to pass the threshold—which seems intentional for a smoke test.

187	def cfgs_get(key, val_config, dataset_name, train_configs, default=None):
188	    """ Try to retrieve a key from the validation set config.

190	    with the same dataset name.

Now I have a clear picture. Let me also check the build_mixture_dataloader call to understand how weights works.

From line 308:

weights = data_config['train'].get('weights', [1.0] * num_trainsets)

The default is [1.0] * num_trainsets if not specified. But in the config, weights: [1.0] is specified with only one value for two datasets. If build_mixture_dataloader expects the same length as the number of iterators, this would be a mismatch. Let me check if this would be a bug.

I need to look at the build_mixture_dataloader signature to see how it actually handles the weights parameter. The critical question is whether it normalizes a single weight value across all datasets or requires the weights list to match the number of data iterators exactly.

Assistant2026-05-27T08:00:34.380Z

Now I can see the key issue with weights: - Line 528: self.sampling_probs = np.array(weights) / sum(weights) - so weights: [1.0] for 2 datasets would normalize to [1.0], but data_iters has 2 elements. When MixtureDataset.__next__ tries to sample, it would pick from the weights, but if the weights array has fewer elements than data_iters, np.random.choice(range(len(self.data_iters)), p=self.sampling_probs) would fail because sampling_probs has only 1 value but there are 2 data_iters.

  • The mismatch is clear: either it tries to sample from 2 data iterators using a probability distribution with only 1 element, which causes a dimension error, or it samples from the weights array itself and always picks the same iterator.

524	class MixtureDataset(IterableDataset):

Now I understand the data format expected by MultiModalDatasetFolder. It looks for: - A root directory - Subdirectories for each modality (e.g., tok_rgb@224/, tok_depth@224/) - Within each modality subdirectory, class folders (like ImageFolder)

This is essentially an ImageFolder-like structure per modality:

/project/data/val/cc12m/
  tok_rgb@224/
    class_name/
      sample_001.npy
      sample_002.npy
      ...
  tok_depth@224/
    class_name/
      sample_001.npy
      ...
  crop_settings/
    class_name/
      sample_001.json
      ...

This is quite different from what you get by untarring webdataset shards. When you untar a WDS shard, you get flat files like:

000000.tok_rgb@224.npy
000000.tok_depth@224.npy
000000.crop_settings.json
000001.tok_rgb@224.npy
...

So just untarring shards won't work directly. The user would need to reorganize the files into the hierarchical structure with modality and class subdirectories.

For a validation set with just a few hundred samples, the practical approach is to untar the shards and write a simple reorganization script. Alternatively, they could use the THINGS dataset as validation to avoid the conversion overhead, though they'd need to be careful about data leakage. Since they already have use_wds: False in their config, they're aware WDS isn't supported for validation—they just need a straightforward way to convert their tar shards into the expected folder layout.

Looking at how MultiModalDatasetFolder works, it expects a standard ImageNet-style directory structure where it discovers classes by scanning subdirectories. So the simplest solution is to untar the shards and reorganize the files into that structure rather than trying to adapt the 4M codebase to support WDS validation.

# Plan: Neural 4M Scaling Experiment Review

## Context
User is running a class project comparing scaling laws for two any-to-any 4M models: a control (RGB↔depth) and a treatment arm (RGB↔depth↔neural recordings). ~300K images, 10% with paired THINGS neural data. $175 Modal budget. Three questions: (1) is the scaling design sound, (2) can validation data use WDS format, (3) are there bugs in the run/config files?

---

## Task 1: Scaling Design Evaluation

### Model Sizes
The four registered models span:
| Config | dim | layers | Est. params |
|--------|-----|--------|-------------|
| `fm_neural_2e_2d_gelu_128_dim` | 128 | 2e+2d | ~7M |
| `fm_neural_2e_2d_gelu_192_dim` | 192 | 2e+2d | ~11M |
| `fm_neural_3e_3d_gelu_256_dim` | 256 | 3e+3d | ~17M |
| `fm_neural_3e_3d_gelu_512_dim` | 512 | 3e+3d | ~44M |

~6× param spread is borderline for scaling laws but acceptable for a class project. One caveat: the two small models use 2-layer architectures and the two large models use 3-layer, so depth is confounded with width. Note this as a limitation.

### Token Budget & Data Repetition
- epoch_size=300,000, tokens/sample=512 → ~153.6M tokens/epoch → **33 epochs** to see 5B tokens
- Each unique image seen ~33 times. With random masking, crop augmentation, and token sampling this is much less severe than pure memorization, but regularization is limited. For a noticeable trend this is fine.
- 3 intermediate evals (indices ≈11, 22, 32) give ~1.7B / 3.4B / 5B token checkpoints, all above the 1B filter → **12 (N,D,loss) data points** per condition for Chinchilla fitting. Good.

### Budget Estimate
- Single A100 @ ~$3.50/hr
- Rough step time: ~10ms (7M model) to ~40ms (44M model)  
- Steps per run: 5e9 / (64×512) ≈ 152,600 steps
- Wall time: ~0.4 hr (tiny) to ~1.7 hr (largest) → ~4.5 hrs per condition × 2 conditions = **~9 GPU hours ≈ $32**
- Well within $175. Budget is comfortable; even doubling estimates leaves headroom.

### Recommendations
- **GPU**: Keep A100. It's the right call—smaller GPUs (L4/A10G) save ~30% cost but risk OOM at larger batch sizes.
- **Batch size**: Consider increasing from 64 → 128 to halve GPU hours. The `blr` already scales linearly with batch size in `run_training_4m.py` (`lr = blr * batch_size / 256`), so `blr: 0.0001` stays correct for either.
- **Run order**: Run the largest model first to validate the full pipeline before committing all budget.
- **`save_ckpt_freq`**: Already set to 2, meaning checkpoints every 2 epochs. Fine for result collection.
- **Fitting**: Chinchilla needs ≥3 points; 12 points is healthy. The mixed-depth design (2e2d vs 3e3d) adds noise to the alpha/beta fit but won't prevent a visible trend.

---

## Task 2: Validation Data in WDS Format

**Short answer: just untar. Don't modify 4M.**

`get_val_dataloader` in `fourm/data/pretrain_utils.py:195` always calls `build_fm_pretraining_dataset` (line 240) regardless of the `use_wds` field—it's silently ignored for val. This calls `MultiModalDatasetFolder` which expects an **ImageFolder-style directory structure** per modality:

```
/project/data/val/cc12m/
  tok_rgb@224/
    samples/          ← one class folder (any name works)
      000000.npy
      000001.npy
      ...
  tok_depth@224/
    samples/
      000000.npy
      ...
  crop_settings/
    samples/
      000000.json
      ...
```

WDS tars extract to flat files like `000000.tok_rgb@224.npy`. A short Python reorganization script handles the conversion:
```python
import tarfile, shutil, os
from pathlib import Path

val_root = Path("/project/data/val/cc12m")
for tar_path in sorted(Path("/project/data/train/cc12m").glob("shard-*.tar")):
    # (pick only your designated val shards)
    with tarfile.open(tar_path) as tar:
        tar.extractall("/tmp/wds_extracted")

for f in Path("/tmp/wds_extracted").iterdir():
    # filename: "000000.tok_rgb@224.npy"
    parts = f.name.split(".", 1)
    modality = parts[1].rsplit(".", 1)[0]   # "tok_rgb@224"
    dest = val_root / modality / "samples" / f.name
    dest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    shutil.move(str(f), dest)
```

Run this once per val shard set; no code changes needed.

---

## Task 3: Bugs

### A. `run_scaling_experiment_2.py`

**Bug 1 (Critical): Wrong path for 3-layer base config** — `line 70`
```python
# WRONG (cfgs/modal/neural vs cfgs/neural/4m/modal)
BASE_MODEL_CFG_3_LAYERS = "/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/modal/neural/4m/model/4m-neural-3e-3d-scaling.yaml"
# CORRECT
BASE_MODEL_CFG_3_LAYERS = "/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/neural/4m/modal/model/4m-neural-3e-3d-scaling.yaml"
```
This causes a `FileNotFoundError` for dim=512 and dim=256 runs.

**Bug 2 (Critical): `extract_model_size` double-appends `/test_run`** — `lines 265-266, 239`
`collect_results` already does `run_dir = run_dir / "test_run"` when `test_run=True`, then passes this modified `run_dir` to `extract_model_size`, which appends `/test_run` again. Fix: remove lines 238-239 from `extract_model_size`.

**Bug 3 (Critical): Wrong args to `run_fit` in "all" mode** — `line 551`
```python
# WRONG
run_fit(RESULTS_FILE, test_run, loss_type)
# CORRECT
run_fit(RESULTS_FILE, SWEEP_OUTPUT_DIR, CONDITION, test_run, loss_type)
```

**Bug 4 (Critical): Wrong args to `plot_results` in `run_fit`** — `line 523`
```python
# WRONG
plot_results(results, law, loss_type)
# CORRECT — also need to thread model_configs through run_fit
plot_results(results, sweep_output_dir, MODEL_CONFIGS, condition, law, loss_type)
```
Add `model_configs=MODEL_CONFIGS` as a parameter to `run_fit`, or reference the global directly.

**Bug 5 (Critical): Wrong result field names in `plot_results` right-axis** — `lines 455-460`
```python
# WRONG
pts = [(r["model_size"], r["loss"]) for r in results if ...]
# CORRECT (keys come from collect_results)
pts = [(r["N"], r[f"loss_{loss_type}"]) for r in results if ...]
```

**Bug 6 (Silent): `--test_run` bool parsing** — `lines 537-540`
`parser.add_argument("--test_run", default=False)` with no type means `--test_run False` stores the string `"False"`, which is truthy. Modal passes `"--test_run", "True"` — works by accident but `"--test_run", "False"` would not disable test mode.
Fix: `parser.add_argument("--test_run", action="store_true", default=False)` and remove `"--test_run", "True"` from `modal_train.py` (or conditionally add it).

**Bug 7 (Harmless): `BASE_DATA_CFG` uses underscore** — `line 72`
`rgb_depth-a0.5.yaml` should be `rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml`. This variable is never used in the code, so no runtime impact.

### B. Data Config (`rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml` and `rgb-depth-a0.5-tiny.yaml`)

**Bug 8 (Silent, significant): `weights: [1.0]` for 2 datasets** — last line of train section
`MixtureDataset.__iter__` (unified_datasets.py:537) does `np.random.choice(len(self.sampling_probs), p=...)`. With `weights=[1.0]` and 2 data iterators, it always samples index 0 (cc12m) and **never samples from things**. The THINGS dataset (which contains your neural recording data) is silently ignored.
```yaml
# WRONG
weights: [1.0]
# CORRECT
weights: [1.0, 1.0]
```
Apply to both `rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml` and `rgb-depth-a0.5-tiny.yaml`.

**Bug 9 (Latent): Relative `alphas_config` path for things dataset** — `rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml:49`
```yaml
alphas_config: "cfgs/neural/4m/alphas_mixture/mix_mod7_all2all_rgb2all_a0.5.yaml"
```
When Modal runs from `cwd=/opt/repo`, this resolves to `/opt/repo/cfgs/...` which doesn't exist (should be `/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/...`). Currently masked by Bug 8 (things is never sampled). After fixing Bug 8, this will crash.
Fix: use absolute path `/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/neural/4m/alphas_mixture/mix_mod7_all2all_rgb2all_a0.5.yaml`.

---

## Approved Plan (edited by user):
# Plan: Neural 4M Scaling Experiment Review

## Context
User is running a class project comparing scaling laws for two any-to-any 4M models: a control (RGB↔depth) and a treatment arm (RGB↔depth↔neural recordings). ~300K images, 10% with paired THINGS neural data. $175 Modal budget. Three questions: (1) is the scaling design sound, (2) can validation data use WDS format, (3) are there bugs in the run/config files?

---

## Task 1: Scaling Design Evaluation

### Model Sizes
The four registered models span:
| Config | dim | layers | Est. params |
|--------|-----|--------|-------------|
| `fm_neural_2e_2d_gelu_128_dim` | 128 | 2e+2d | ~7M |
| `fm_neural_2e_2d_gelu_192_dim` | 192 | 2e+2d | ~11M |
| `fm_neural_3e_3d_gelu_256_dim` | 256 | 3e+3d | ~17M |
| `fm_neural_3e_3d_gelu_512_dim` | 512 | 3e+3d | ~44M |

~6× param spread is borderline for scaling laws but acceptable for a class project. One caveat: the two small models use 2-layer architectures and the two large models use 3-layer, so depth is confounded with width. Note this as a limitation.

### Token Budget & Data Repetition
- epoch_size=300,000, tokens/sample=512 → ~153.6M tokens/epoch → **33 epochs** to see 5B tokens
- Each unique image seen ~33 times. With random masking, crop augmentation, and token sampling this is much less severe than pure memorization, but regularization is limited. For a noticeable trend this is fine.
- 3 intermediate evals (indices ≈11, 22, 32) give ~1.7B / 3.4B / 5B token checkpoints, all above the 1B filter → **12 (N,D,loss) data points** per condition for Chinchilla fitting. Good.

### Budget Estimate
- Single A100 @ ~$3.50/hr
- Rough step time: ~10ms (7M model) to ~40ms (44M model)  
- Steps per run: 5e9 / (64×512) ≈ 152,600 steps
- Wall time: ~0.4 hr (tiny) to ~1.7 hr (largest) → ~4.5 hrs per condition × 2 conditions = **~9 GPU hours ≈ $32**
- Well within $175. Budget is comfortable; even doubling estimates leaves headroom.

### Recommendations
- **GPU**: Keep A100. It's the right call—smaller GPUs (L4/A10G) save ~30% cost but risk OOM at larger batch sizes.
- **Batch size**: Consider increasing from 64 → 128 to halve GPU hours. The `blr` already scales linearly with batch size in `run_training_4m.py` (`lr = blr * batch_size / 256`), so `blr: 0.0001` stays correct for either.
- **Run order**: Run the largest model first to validate the full pipeline before committing all budget.
- **`save_ckpt_freq`**: Already set to 2, meaning checkpoints every 2 epochs. Fine for result collection.
- **Fitting**: Chinchilla needs ≥3 points; 12 points is healthy. The mixed-depth design (2e2d vs 3e3d) adds noise to the alpha/beta fit but won't prevent a visible trend.

---

## Task 2: Validation Data in WDS Format

**Short answer: just untar. Don't modify 4M.**

`get_val_dataloader` in `fourm/data/pretrain_utils.py:195` always calls `build_fm_pretraining_dataset` (line 240) regardless of the `use_wds` field—it's silently ignored for val. This calls `MultiModalDatasetFolder` which expects an **ImageFolder-style directory structure** per modality:

```
/project/data/val/cc12m/
  tok_rgb@224/
    samples/          ← one class folder (any name works)
      000000.npy
      000001.npy
      ...
  tok_depth@224/
    samples/
      000000.npy
      ...
  crop_settings/
    samples/
      000000.json
      ...
```

WDS tars extract to flat files like `000000.tok_rgb@224.npy`. A short Python reorganization script handles the conversion:
```python
import tarfile, shutil, os
from pathlib import Path

val_root = Path("/project/data/val/cc12m")
for tar_path in sorted(Path("/project/data/train/cc12m").glob("shard-*.tar")):
    # (pick only your designated val shards)
    with tarfile.open(tar_path) as tar:
        tar.extractall("/tmp/wds_extracted")

for f in Path("/tmp/wds_extracted").iterdir():
    # filename: "000000.tok_rgb@224.npy"
    parts = f.name.split(".", 1)
    modality = parts[1].rsplit(".", 1)[0]   # "tok_rgb@224"
    dest = val_root / modality / "samples" / f.name
    dest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    shutil.move(str(f), dest)
```

Run this once per val shard set; no code changes needed.

---

## Task 3: Bugs

### A. `run_scaling_experiment_2.py`

**Bug 1 (Critical): Wrong path for 3-layer base config** — `line 70`
```python
# WRONG (cfgs/modal/neural vs cfgs/neural/4m/modal)

# CORRECT
BASE_MODEL_CFG_3_LAYERS = "/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/neural/4m/modal/model/4m-neural-3e-3d-scaling.yaml"
```
This causes a `FileNotFoundError` for dim=512 and dim=256 runs.

**Bug 2 (Critical): `extract_model_size` double-appends `/test_run`** — `lines 265-266, 239`

```python

```

**Bug 5 (Critical): Wrong result field names in `plot_results` right-axis** — `lines 455-460`
```python

```

**Bug 6 (Silent): `--test_run` bool parsing** — `lines 537-540`
`parser.add_argument("--test_run", default=False)` with no type means `--test_run False` stores the string `"False"`, which is truthy. Modal passes `"--test_run", "True"` — works by accident but `"--test_run", "False"` would not disable test mode.
Fix: `parser.add_argument("--test_run", action="store_true", default=False)` and remove `"--test_run", "True"` from `modal_train.py` (or conditionally add it).

**Bug 7 (Harmless): `BASE_DATA_CFG` uses underscore** — `line 72`
`rgb_depth-a0.5.yaml` should be `rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml`. This variable is never used in the code, so no runtime impact.

### B. Data Config (`rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml` and `rgb-depth-a0.5-tiny.yaml`)

**Bug 8 (Silent, significant): `weights: [1.0]` for 2 datasets** — last line of train section
`MixtureDataset.__iter__` (unified_datasets.py:537) does `np.random.choice(len(self.sampling_probs), p=...)`. With `weights=[1.0]` and 2 data iterators, it always samples index 0 (cc12m) and **never samples from things**. The THINGS dataset (which contains your neural recording data) is silently ignored.
```yaml

# CORRECT

```
Apply to both `rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml` and `rgb-depth-a0.5-tiny.yaml`.

**Bug 9 (Latent): Relative `alphas_config` path for things dataset** — `rgb-depth-a0.5.yaml:49`
```yaml

```
When Modal runs from `cwd=/opt/repo`, this resolves to `/opt/repo/cfgs/...` which doesn't exist (should be `/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/...`). Currently masked by Bug 8 (things is never sampled). After fixing Bug 8, this will crash.
Fix: use absolute path `/opt/repo/ml-4m/cfgs/neural/4m/alphas_mixture/mix_mod7_all2all_rgb2all_a0.5.yaml`.

Assistant2026-05-27T08:23:57.409Z

Here's a summary of everything found and fixed:

Task 1 — Scaling Design

Your setup is sound for a class project. Key numbers: - 4 model sizes (~7M → 44M params, ~6× spread) is borderline but will show a visible trend - 5B tokens / 33 epochs gives clear signal; 3 intermediate eval points per run → 12 (N,D,loss) data points for Chinchilla, which is healthy - Budget: single A100 sweep of both conditions should cost ~$30–80 even with generous overhead — well inside $175 - Recommendation: keep A100, keep batch_size: 64. If you want to cut time in half, bump to batch_size: 128 — the blr linear scaling in the training script handles the LR adjustment automatically - Caveat: dim 128/192 use 2-layer and dim 256/512 use 3-layer, so depth is confounded with width. Worth one sentence in the write-up

Task 2 — Validation Data Format

Don't modify 4M. get_val_dataloader in pretrain_utils.py:240 always calls build_fm_pretraining_dataset regardless of use_wds. The expected structure is an ImageFolder-style layout per modality:

/project/data/val/cc12m/
  tok_rgb@224/samples/000000.npy ...
  tok_depth@224/samples/000000.npy ...
  crop_settings/samples/000000.json ...

Untar your val shards and run the reorganization script from the plan to get there.

Task 3 — Bugs Fixed

# Severity File Description
1 Critical run_scaling_experiment_2.py:70 BASE_MODEL_CFG_3_LAYERS had cfgs/modal/neural instead of cfgs/neural/4m/modal → FileNotFoundError on dim=512/256 runs

6 Silent run_scaling_experiment_2.py:534 + modal_train.py:64 --test_run stored a string, so "False" would be truthy; changed to action="store_true"; modal_train.py now only appends the flag when dryrun=True
7 Harmless run_scaling_experiment_2.py:72 BASE_DATA_CFG had underscore in filename (unused variable)

50	def _make_tar(path: Path, entries: list[tuple[str, str, bytes]]) -> None:
51	    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
52	    with tarfile.open(path, "w") as tar:
53	        for key, ext, data in entries:
54	            info = tarfile.TarInfo(name=f"{key}.{ext}")
55	            info.size = len(data)
56	            tar.addfile(info, io.BytesIO(data))
57	
58	
59	def _npy_bytes(arr: np.ndarray) -> bytes:
60	    buf = io.BytesIO()
61	    np.save(buf, arr, allow_pickle=False)
62	    return buf.getvalue()

65	def run_demo() -> None:
66	    """Build a synthetic shard and walk samples through the 4M decode path."""
67	    import webdataset as wds
68	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import (
69	        filter_metadata,
70	        multi_tarfile_samples,
71	        remove_extensions,
72	        tok_to_int64,
73	        wds_decoder,
74	    )
75	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import map as keyless_map
76	
77	    from fourm_neural_transforms import EegTokTransform, MegTokTransform
78	
79	    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:
80	        root = Path(tmp) / "things"
81	        ids = ["000000001", "000000002", "000000003"]
82	
83	        rgb_arr = lambda i: np.full((TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,), int(i), dtype=np.int16)
84	        depth_arr = np.zeros((TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,), dtype=np.int16)
85	        meg_real = np.full((4, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), 7, dtype=np.int16)
86	        meg_sentinel = np.full((1, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
87	        eeg_real = np.full((2, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), 3, dtype=np.int16)
88	        eeg_sentinel = np.full((1, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
89	        mask_real = np.array([1], dtype=np.uint8)
90	        mask_zero = np.array([0], dtype=np.uint8)
91	
92	        for mod, arrs in [
93	            ("tok_rgb", [(i, _npy_bytes(rgb_arr(i))) for i in ids]),
94	            ("tok_depth", [(i, _npy_bytes(depth_arr)) for i in ids]),
95	            (
96	                "tok_meg",
97	                [
98	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(meg_real)),
99	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(meg_sentinel)),
100	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(meg_real)),
101	                ],
102	            ),
103	            (
104	                "tok_eeg",
105	                [
106	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(eeg_real)),
107	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(eeg_sentinel)),
108	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(eeg_real)),
109	                ],
110	            ),
111	            (
112	                "meg_mask",
113	                [
114	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
115	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(mask_zero)),
116	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
117	                ],
118	            ),
119	            (
120	                "eeg_mask",
121	                [
122	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
123	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(mask_zero)),
124	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
125	                ],
126	            ),
127	        ]:
128	            _make_tar(
129	                root / f"{mod}/shard_000.tar",
130	                [(k, "npy", b) for k, b in arrs],
131	            )
132	
133	        url = (
134	            f"{root}/[tok_rgb,tok_depth,tok_meg,tok_eeg,meg_mask,eeg_mask]/"
135	            "shard_000.tar"
136	        )
137	        print(f"data_path = {url}\n")
138	
139	        pipeline = wds.DataPipeline(
140	            wds.SimpleShardList(url),
141	            partial(multi_tarfile_samples, handler=lambda e: (_ for _ in ()).throw(e)),
142	            wds.decode(wds_decoder),
143	            wds.map(remove_extensions),
144	            keyless_map(filter_metadata),
145	            keyless_map(tok_to_int64),
146	        )
147	
148	        print("=" * 72)
149	        print("  4M pipeline output (after decode + filter)")
150	        print("=" * 72)
151	        for sample in pipeline:
152	            shapes = {
153	                k: getattr(v, "shape", type(v).__name__) for k, v in sample.items()
154	            }
155	            print(f"  modalities = {sorted(sample)}")
156	            print(f"  shapes     = {shapes}")
157	            print()
158	
159	        print("=" * 72)
160	        print("  After trial transforms")
161	        print("=" * 72)
162	        meg_tx = MegTokTransform(training=True, seed=0)
163	        eeg_tx = EegTokTransform(training=True, seed=0)
164	        for label, arr, tx in [
165	            ("MEG real", meg_real, meg_tx),
166	            ("MEG sentinel", meg_sentinel, meg_tx),
167	            ("EEG real", eeg_real, eeg_tx),
168	            ("EEG sentinel", eeg_sentinel, eeg_tx),
169	        ]:
170	            tokens = tx.preprocess(arr)
171	            print(f"  {label:>14s}: in={tuple(arr.shape)} -> out={tuple(tokens.shape)}")

174	def _load_configs(config_path: Path) -> tuple[dict[str, Any], dict[str, Any], dict[str, Any]]:
175	    """Return (main_cfg, train_ds_cfg, val_ds_cfg_or_empty). Accepts main or data yaml."""
176	    import yaml
177	
178	    config_path = config_path.resolve()
179	    if not config_path.is_absolute():
180	        config_path = (_REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
181	
182	    with open(config_path) as f:
183	        cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
184	
185	    if "train" in cfg and "datasets" in cfg.get("train", {}):
186	        main = {
187	            "input_size": THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
188	            "num_input_tokens": 256,
189	            "num_target_tokens": 256,
190	            "batch_size": 4,
191	            "epoch_size": 64,
192	            "text_tokenizer_path": str(repo_paths.TEXT_TOKENIZER),
193	        }
194	        train_ds = next(iter(cfg["train"]["datasets"].values()))
195	        val_ds = {}
196	        if "val" in cfg and cfg["val"].get("datasets"):
197	            val_ds = next(iter(cfg["val"]["datasets"].values()))
198	        return main, train_ds, val_ds
199	
200	    data_rel = cfg.get("data_config")
201	    if not data_rel:
202	        raise ValueError(f"{config_path}: expected data_config or train.datasets")
203	    data_path = Path(data_rel)
204	    if not data_path.is_absolute():
205	        data_path = (_REPO_ROOT / data_path).resolve()
206	    with open(data_path) as f:
207	        data_cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
208	    train_ds = next(iter(data_cfg["train"]["datasets"].values()))
209	    val_ds = {}
210	    if "val" in data_cfg and data_cfg["val"].get("datasets"):
211	        val_ds = next(iter(data_cfg["val"]["datasets"].values()))
212	    return cfg, train_ds, val_ds

227	def _build_modality_info(
228	    all_domain_names: list[str],
229	    input_size: int = THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
230	) -> dict:
231	    import copy
232	
233	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
234	
235	    # Model + masking only need in/out token domains, not presence flags.
236	    token_domains = [d for d in all_domain_names if not d.endswith("_mask")]
237	    modality_info = {
238	        mod: copy.deepcopy(MODALITY_INFO[mod])
239	        for mod in token_domains
240	        if mod in MODALITY_INFO
241	    }
242	    for mod, info in modality_info.items():
243	        if info.get("type") == "img":
244	            patch_size = info.get("patch_size", THINGS_PATCH_SIZE)
245	            info["max_tokens"] = pretoken_grid_num_tokens(input_size, patch_size)
246	    return modality_info
247	
248	
249	def _iterate_loader(loader, n_batches: int, label: str) -> None:
250	    print(f"{label}: iterating {n_batches} batches…\n")
251	    for i, batch in enumerate(loader):
252	        if i >= n_batches:
253	            break
254	        print(f"batch {i}: keys = {sorted(batch.keys())}")
255	        for k, v in batch.items():
256	            if isinstance(v, dict) and "tensor" in v:
257	                print(f"  {k:>16s} : tensor shape={tuple(v['tensor'].shape)}")
258	            else:
259	                shape = getattr(v, "shape", None)
260	                print(
261	                    f"  {k:>16s} : shape={tuple(shape) if shape is not None else type(v).__name__}"
262	                )
263	        print()
264

266	# Stock mixture loader computes epoch_size // (num_gpus * num_workers * batch_size),
267	# so the dryrun cannot use 0 workers. One worker keeps it cheap and single-process.
268	_DRYRUN_NUM_WORKERS = 1
269	
270	
271	def run_dryrun(config_path: Path, n_batches: int = 4) -> None:
272	    """Build train + val dataloaders and iterate a few batches."""
273	    from tokenizers import Tokenizer
274	
275	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
276	    from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import get_train_dataloader, get_val_dataloader, setup_sampling_mod_info
277	
278	    main_cfg, train_ds, val_ds = _load_configs(config_path)
279	    input_size = main_cfg.get("input_size", THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)
280	
281	    in_domains = sorted(train_ds["in_domains"].split("-"))
282	    out_domains = sorted(train_ds["out_domains"].split("-"))
283	    all_domains = sorted(set(in_domains) | set(out_domains))
284	    modality_info_full = _build_modality_info(all_domains, input_size)
285	    mod_info, sampling_weights = setup_sampling_mod_info(train_ds, modality_info_full)
286	
287	    tok_path = main_cfg.get("text_tokenizer_path", str(repo_paths.TEXT_TOKENIZER))
288	    text_tokenizer = Tokenizer.from_file(tok_path)
289	
290	    train_loader = get_train_dataloader(
291	        dataset_config=train_ds,
292	        modality_info=mod_info,
293	        sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
294	        text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
295	        input_size=input_size,
296	        num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
297	        num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
298	        min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
299	        min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
300	        num_tasks=1,
301	        num_workers=_DRYRUN_NUM_WORKERS,
302	        dataset_batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
303	        epoch_size=main_cfg.get("epoch_size", max(n_batches * 4, 16)),
304	    )
305	    _iterate_loader(train_loader, n_batches, "train dryrun")
306	
307	    if val_ds.get("data_path"):
308	        val_loader = get_val_dataloader(
309	            dataset_config=val_ds,
310	            dataset_name="things",
311	            train_configs={"things": train_ds},
312	            modality_info=mod_info,
313	            sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
314	            text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
315	            input_size=input_size,
316	            num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
317	            num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
318	            min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
319	            min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
320	            fixed_eval=False,
321	            fixed_eval_input_tokens=128,
322	            fixed_eval_target_tokens=128,
323	            dist_eval=False,
324	            num_tasks=1,
325	            num_workers=0,
326	            batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
327	            pin_mem=False,
328	        )
329	        _iterate_loader(val_loader, n_batches, "val dryrun")
330	
331	
332	def _clean_extra_argv(extra_argv: list[str]) -> list[str]:
333	    """Drop the leading ``--`` separator argparse.REMAINDER keeps.
334	
335	    ``train --config X -- --data_config Y`` captures ``['--', '--data_config', Y]``.
336	    The 4M trainer's argparse treats a forwarded ``--`` as a positional and errors
337	    ("unrecognized arguments"), so strip exactly the one leading separator.
338	    """
339	    if extra_argv and extra_argv[0] == "--":
340	        return extra_argv[1:]
341	    return extra_argv
342	
343	
344	def run_train(config_path: Path, extra_argv: list[str]) -> None:
345	    """Hand off to 4M's official trainer with neural patches active."""
346	    import os
347	    import runpy
348	
349	    extra_argv = _clean_extra_argv(extra_argv)
350	
351	    # Stock run_training_4m.py always uses DDP; set single-process vars if missing.
352	    os.environ.setdefault("RANK", "0")
353	    os.environ.setdefault("WORLD_SIZE", "1")
354	    os.environ.setdefault("LOCAL_RANK", "0")
355	    os.environ.setdefault("MASTER_ADDR", "127.0.0.1")
356	    os.environ.setdefault("MASTER_PORT", "29500")
357	
358	    ml_4m_root = repo_paths.ML4M_DIR
359	    if not (ml_4m_root / "run_training_4m.py").exists():
360	        raise FileNotFoundError(
361	            f"4M trainer not found at {ml_4m_root}. "
362	            "Install with: pip install -e external/ml-4m"
363	        )
364	    sys.path.insert(0, str(ml_4m_root))
365	    config_path = config_path.resolve()
366	    if not config_path.is_absolute():
367	        config_path = (_REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
368	
369	    # Stock run_training_4m.py defaults --text_tokenizer_path to a cwd-relative path that
370	    # does not exist outside the 4M checkout (e.g. on Modal). Realize the configs'
371	    # "auto-derived from FOURM_ML4M_DIR" promise: inject the resolved tokenizer unless the
372	    # config or caller already provides one. (CLI args override the config's defaults.)
373	    import yaml
374	
375	    with open(config_path) as f:
376	        _main_cfg = yaml.safe_load(f) or {}
377	    if "--text_tokenizer_path" not in extra_argv and not _main_cfg.get("text_tokenizer_path"):
378	        extra_argv = [*extra_argv, "--text_tokenizer_path", str(repo_paths.TEXT_TOKENIZER)]
379	
380	    sys.argv = ["run_training_4m.py", "-c", str(config_path), *extra_argv]
381	    print(f"handing off to 4M trainer: argv = {sys.argv}\n")
382	    try:
383	        runpy.run_path(str(ml_4m_root / "run_training_4m.py"), run_name="__main__")
384	    finally:
385	        # Stock trainer inits the process group but never tears it down; doing it
386	        # here avoids the "destroy_process_group() was not called" NCCL warning.
387	        import torch.distributed as dist
388	
389	        if dist.is_available() and dist.is_initialized():
390	            dist.destroy_process_group()
391	
392	
393	def main() -> None:
394	    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
395	        description=__doc__,
396	        formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,
397	    )
398	    sub = p.add_subparsers(dest="mode", required=True)
399	
400	    sub.add_parser("demo", help="Synthetic shard pipeline walkthrough.")
401	
402	    p_dry = sub.add_parser("dryrun", help="Iterate train + val batches from config.")
403	    p_dry.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
404	    p_dry.add_argument("--n-batches", type=int, default=4)
405	
406	    p_train = sub.add_parser("train", help="Run 4M run_training_4m.py.")
407	    p_train.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
408	    p_train.add_argument("extra", nargs=argparse.REMAINDER)
409	
410	    p_val = sub.add_parser("validate", help="Check main/data YAML against 4M (no GPU/data).")
411	    p_val.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
412	
413	    args = p.parse_args()
414	    if args.mode == "demo":
415	        run_demo()
416	    elif args.mode == "dryrun":
417	        run_dryrun(args.config, args.n_batches)
418	    elif args.mode == "validate":
419	        run_validate(args.config)
420	    elif args.mode == "train":
421	        run_train(args.config, args.extra or [])
422	
423	
424	if __name__ == "__main__":
425	    main()

Tool reply2026-05-28T02:00:46.149Z
1	"""Minimal hooks so stock 4M dataloaders work with THINGS neural shards.
2	
3	We do **not** reimplement the WebDataset pipeline. Instead we patch three
4	integration points and delegate everything else to upstream 4M:
5	
6	  * ``UnifiedMasking`` → ``PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking`` (meg/eeg absence)
7	  * ``PreTokenizedImageAugmenter`` → ``ThingsImageAugmenter`` (optional crop_settings)
8	  * ``get_val_dataloader`` → WDS branch when ``use_wds: true`` (stock val is folder-only)
9	
10	Train uses stock ``get_train_dataloader`` → ``build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader`` unchanged.
11	Neural transforms are stock ``AbstractTransform`` subclasses registered in
12	``MODALITY_TRANSFORMS`` via ``fourm_neural_modalities``.
13	"""
14	
15	from __future__ import annotations
16	
17	import copy
18	from functools import partial
19	
20	import webdataset as wds
21	from fourm.data import pretrain_utils
22	from fourm.data import unified_datasets as ud
23	from fourm.data import image_augmenter as ia
24	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import CropSettingsTransform, IdentityTransform
25	from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import cfgs_get
26	from fourm.data.unified_datasets import (
27	    default_collate,
28	    filter_metadata,
29	    map,
30	    multi_tarfile_samples,
31	    remove_extensions,
32	    rename_modalities,
33	    tok_to_int64,
34	    wds_decoder,
35	)
36	import torchvision.transforms as transforms
37	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import UnifiedDataTransform
38	
39	import fourm_neural_modalities
40	from neural_masking import PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
41	from things_augmenter import ThingsImageAugmenter
42	
43	_PRESENCE_PATHS = {"meg_mask": "meg_mask", "eeg_mask": "eeg_mask"}
44	
45	# Picks ONE trial per sample and splits it into the neural output heads (coherent across
46	# the 4 MEG RVQ layers). None until a loader is built; set for train vs eval trial sampling.
47	_NEURAL_SPLITTER = None
48	
49	_ORIG_UNIFIED_MASKING = ud.UnifiedMasking
50	_ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG = ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter
51	_ORIG_GET_VAL = pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader
52	_ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES = ud.rename_modalities
53	_PATCHED = False
54	
55	
56	class _SeqSafeRandom:
57	    """Proxy for the stdlib ``random`` module that lists ``sample`` populations.
58	
59	    Stock 4M's decoder does ``random.sample(mod_dict.items(), …)``; ``random.sample``
60	    rejected dict views / sets starting in Python 3.11. Swapping ``fm.random`` for
61	    this proxy keeps the model forward working on 3.11+ without editing ``ml-4m`` —
62	    every other attribute delegates to the real module unchanged.
63	    """
64	
65	    def __init__(self, real):
66	        self._real = real
67	
68	    def sample(self, population, k):
69	        return self._real.sample(list(population), k)
70	
71	    def __getattr__(self, name):
72	        return getattr(self._real, name)
73	
74	
75	def _set_neural_target_splitter(training: bool) -> None:
76	    """Install the per-sample neural-output trial splitter (train vs eval sampling)."""
77	    global _NEURAL_SPLITTER
78	    from neural_trial_transform import NeuralTargetSplitter
79	
80	    _NEURAL_SPLITTER = NeuralTargetSplitter(training=training)
81	
82	
83	def _rename_modalities(sample, modality_paths):
84	    """Stock rename assumes every path exists; THINGS omits optional ``crop_settings`` tars.
85	
86	    Also the single point where neural OUTPUT heads are materialized: rename fans the
87	    ``tok_meg`` / ``tok_eeg`` folder out to the output modalities (aliasing one array),
88	    then the splitter picks one trial and slices the per-head targets — so the 4 MEG RVQ
89	    heads stay coherent. No-op when no neural output modality is requested.
90	    """
91	    present = {out: src for out, src in modality_paths.items() if src in sample}
92	    if not present:
93	        return sample
94	    renamed = _ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES(sample, present)
95	    if _NEURAL_SPLITTER is not None:
96	        _NEURAL_SPLITTER(renamed)
97	    return renamed
98	
99	
100	def _extend_modality_paths(modality_info: dict) -> dict[str, str]:
101	    paths = {mod: modality_info[mod].get("path", None) or mod for mod in modality_info}
102	    paths.update(_PRESENCE_PATHS)
103	    return paths
104	
105	
106	def _wds_eval_loader(
107	    data_path: str,
108	    all_domains: list[str],
109	    modality_info: dict,
110	    modality_transforms: dict,
111	    image_augmenter,
112	    text_tokenizer,
113	    input_tokens_range,
114	    target_tokens_range,
115	    num_workers: int,
116	    batch_size: int,
117	    sampling_weights=None,
118	    modality_name_map=None,
119	):
120	    """Deterministic WDS val loader — only gap stock 4M does not cover.
121	
122	    Reuses the same transform stack as ``build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader``
123	    (``UnifiedDataTransform`` + patched ``PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking``).
124	    Pipeline differs only in shard source (``SimpleShardList``, no shuffle/repeat).
125	    """
126	    fourm_neural_modalities.register(training=False)
127	    _set_neural_target_splitter(training=False)  # eval: deterministic trial 0
128	
129	    modality_paths = _extend_modality_paths(modality_info)
130	    modality_transforms = copy.deepcopy(modality_transforms)
131	    if any(modality_info[d].get("pretokenized", False) for d in all_domains):
132	        modality_transforms["crop_settings"] = CropSettingsTransform()
133	    modality_transforms["__key__"] = IdentityTransform()
134	
135	    transform = transforms.Compose(
136	        [
137	            UnifiedDataTransform(
138	                transforms_dict=modality_transforms,
139	                image_augmenter=image_augmenter,
140	            ),
141	            PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(
142	                modality_info=modality_info,
143	                text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
144	                input_tokens_range=input_tokens_range,
145	                target_tokens_range=target_tokens_range,
146	                sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
147	            ),
148	        ]
149	    )
150	
151	    datapipe = wds.DataPipeline(
152	        wds.SimpleShardList(data_path),
153	        partial(multi_tarfile_samples, modality_name_map=modality_name_map),
154	        wds.decode(wds_decoder),
155	        wds.map(remove_extensions),
156	        map(filter_metadata),
157	        map(tok_to_int64),
158	        # Tolerant rename: a task's shards may omit optional folders (e.g. meg_mask
159	        # for a vision-only val task), so skip paths not present in the sample.
160	        map(partial(_rename_modalities, modality_paths=modality_paths)),
161	        map(transform),
162	        wds.batched(batch_size, collation_fn=default_collate, partial=False),
163	    )
164	    return wds.WebLoader(datapipe, num_workers=num_workers, batch_size=None)
165	
166	
167	def _neural_get_val_dataloader(
168	    dataset_config,
169	    dataset_name,
170	    train_configs,
171	    modality_info,
172	    sampling_weights,
173	    text_tokenizer,
174	    input_size,
175	    num_input_tokens,
176	    num_target_tokens,
177	    min_input_tokens,
178	    min_target_tokens,
179	    fixed_eval,
180	    fixed_eval_input_tokens,
181	    fixed_eval_target_tokens,
182	    dist_eval,
183	    num_tasks,
184	    num_workers,
185	    batch_size,
186	    pin_mem,
187	):
188	    """Stock val loader, plus WDS tars when ``use_wds: true`` in val config."""
189	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
190	    from fourm.data.modality_transforms import CaptionTransform
191	    from fourm.data.image_augmenter import CenterCropImageAugmenter
192	
193	    dataset_type = cfgs_get("type", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs)
194	    use_wds = cfgs_get("use_wds", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs, False)
195	
196	    if not (dataset_type == "multimodal" and use_wds):
197	        return _ORIG_GET_VAL(
198	            dataset_config,
199	            dataset_name,
200	            train_configs,
201	            modality_info,
202	            sampling_weights,
203	            text_tokenizer,
204	            input_size,
205	            num_input_tokens,
206	            num_target_tokens,
207	            min_input_tokens,
208	            min_target_tokens,
209	            fixed_eval,
210	            fixed_eval_input_tokens,
211	            fixed_eval_target_tokens,
212	            dist_eval,
213	            num_tasks,
214	            num_workers,
215	            batch_size,
216	            pin_mem,
217	        )
218	
219	    in_domains = sorted(
220	        cfgs_get("in_domains", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs).split("-")
221	    )
222	    out_domains = sorted(
223	        cfgs_get("out_domains", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs).split("-")
224	    )
225	    all_domains = sorted(set(in_domains) | set(out_domains))
226	
227	    modality_transforms = MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
228	    if "caption" in modality_transforms:
229	        modality_transforms["caption"] = CaptionTransform(
230	            aligned_captions=cfgs_get(
231	                "aligned_captions", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs, True
232	            )
233	        )
234	
235	    main_augment_domain = cfgs_get(
236	        "main_augment_domain", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs
237	    )
238	    is_pretokenized = any(
239	        modality_info[mod].get("pretokenized", False) for mod in modality_info
240	    )
241	    eval_image_augmenter = (
242	        ThingsImageAugmenter(
243	            target_size=input_size, no_aug=True, main_domain=main_augment_domain
244	        )
245	        if is_pretokenized
246	        else CenterCropImageAugmenter(
247	            target_size=input_size, main_domain=main_augment_domain
248	        )
249	    )
250	
251	    if fixed_eval:
252	        input_tokens_range = (fixed_eval_input_tokens, fixed_eval_input_tokens)
253	        target_tokens_range = (fixed_eval_target_tokens, fixed_eval_target_tokens)
254	    else:
255	        num_input_tokens = dataset_config.get("num_input_tokens", num_input_tokens)
256	        num_target_tokens = dataset_config.get("num_target_tokens", num_target_tokens)
257	        min_input_tokens = dataset_config.get("min_input_tokens", min_input_tokens)
258	        min_target_tokens = dataset_config.get("min_target_tokens", min_target_tokens)
259	        min_input_tokens = (
260	            num_input_tokens if min_input_tokens is None else min_input_tokens
261	        )
262	        min_target_tokens = (
263	            num_target_tokens if min_target_tokens is None else min_target_tokens
264	        )
265	        input_tokens_range = (min_input_tokens, num_input_tokens)
266	        target_tokens_range = (min_target_tokens, num_target_tokens)
267	
268	    print(
269	        "Warning: Eval stats may vary slightly as the masking applied on images is random."
270	    )
271	    return _wds_eval_loader(
272	        data_path=cfgs_get("data_path", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs),
273	        all_domains=all_domains,
274	        modality_info=modality_info,
275	        modality_transforms=modality_transforms,
276	        image_augmenter=eval_image_augmenter,
277	        text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
278	        input_tokens_range=input_tokens_range,
279	        target_tokens_range=target_tokens_range,
280	        num_workers=num_workers,
281	        batch_size=batch_size,
282	        sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
283	        modality_name_map=cfgs_get(
284	            "modality_name_map", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs
285	        ),
286	    )
287	
288	
289	def patch_pretrain_utils() -> None:
290	    """Install neural hooks into stock 4M (idempotent)."""
291	    global _PATCHED
292	    if _PATCHED:
293	        return
294	
295	    # Stock WDS + folder datasets instantiate these classes by reference.
296	    ud.UnifiedMasking = PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
297	    ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = ThingsImageAugmenter
298	    pretrain_utils.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = ThingsImageAugmenter
299	    ud.rename_modalities = _rename_modalities
300	
301	    # Make the decoder forward's random.sample(dict.items()) work on Python 3.11+.
302	    from fourm.models import fm as _fm
303	
304	    if not isinstance(_fm.random, _SeqSafeRandom):
305	        _fm.random = _SeqSafeRandom(_fm.random)
306	
307	    fourm_neural_modalities.register(training=True)
308	    _set_neural_target_splitter(training=True)  # train: random trial per sample
309	
310	    pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader = _neural_get_val_dataloader
311	    import fourm.data as fd
312	
313	    fd.get_val_dataloader = _neural_get_val_dataloader
314	    _PATCHED = True
315	
316	
317	def unpatch_pretrain_utils() -> None:
318	    """Restore stock 4M (for tests)."""
319	    global _PATCHED, _NEURAL_SPLITTER
320	    _NEURAL_SPLITTER = None
321	    ud.UnifiedMasking = _ORIG_UNIFIED_MASKING
322	    ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = _ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG
323	    pretrain_utils.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = _ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG
324	    ud.rename_modalities = _ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES
325	    pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader = _ORIG_GET_VAL
326	    import fourm.data as fd
327	
328	    fd.get_val_dataloader = _ORIG_GET_VAL
329	
330	    from fourm.models import fm as _fm
331	
332	    if isinstance(_fm.random, _SeqSafeRandom):
333	        _fm.random = _fm.random._real
334	    _PATCHED = False
